-00002450: 5468 6520 7079 336f 2072 6570 6f72 7469  The py3o reporti

-000024f0: 733d 2273 696d 706c 6522 3e0a 3c6c 693e  s="simple">.<li>
-00002500: 7468 6520 7265 706f 7274 2069 7320 6372  the report is cr

-00002520: 6f66 6669 6365 2028 4f44 5420 6f72 204f  office (ODT or O

-00002610: 582c 2044 6f63 626f 6f6b 2c20 584c 532c  X, Docbook, XLS,

-00002630: 3e0a 3c70 3e54 6865 206b 6579 2061 6476  >.<p>The key adv
-00002640: 616e 7461 6765 7320 6f66 2061 204c 6962  antages of a Lib
-00002650: 7265 6f66 6669 6365 2062 6173 6564 2072  reoffice based r

+00002600: 2f6c 693e 0a3c 2f75 6c3e 0a3c 703e 5468  /li>.</ul>.<p>Th
+00002610: 6520 6b65 7920 6164 7661 6e74 6167 6573  e key advantages
+00002620: 206f 6620 6120 4c69 6272 656f 6666 6963   of a Libreoffic
+00002630: 6520 6261 7365 6420 7265 706f 7274 696e  e based reportin
+00002640: 6720 656e 6769 6e65 2061 7265 3a3c 2f70  g engine are:</p
+00002650: 3e0a 3c75 6c20 636c 6173 733d 2273 696d  >.<ul class="sim

+00002720: 0a3c 6c69 3e46 6f72 2061 2050 4446 2072  .<li>For a PDF r
+00002730: 6570 6f72 7420 696e 2041 342f 4c65 7474  eport in A4/Lett

+000029b0: 2f75 6c3e 0a3c 703e 5468 6973 206d 6f64  /ul>.<p>This mod
+000029c0: 756c 6520 3c65 6d3e 7265 706f 7274 5f70  ule <em>report_p

+000029e0: 6261 7365 206d 6f64 756c 6520 666f 7220  base module for 
+000029f0: 7468 6520 5079 336f 2072 6570 6f72 7469  the Py3o reporti
+00002a00: 6e67 2065 6e67 696e 652e 2049 6620 7573  ng engine. If us
+00002a10: 6564 2061 6c6f 6e65 2c20 6974 2077 696c  ed alone, it wil

+00002a70: 636f 6e76 6572 7369 6f6e 2e20 5468 6973  conversion. This
+00002a80: 2069 7320 736c 6f77 2061 6e64 2063 616e   is slow and can

+00002cf0: 0a3c 703e 5468 6973 2072 6570 6f72 7469  .<p>This reporti

+00002de0: 2e20 596f 7520 6361 6e6e 6f74 2075 7365  . You cannot use
